# Problem 3188

- Domain: `coding`

## Problem

```text
There are n teams numbered from 0 to n - 1 in a tournament.
Given a 0-indexed 2D boolean matrix grid of size n * n. For all i, j that 0 <= i, j <= n - 1 and i != j team i is stronger than team j if grid[i][j] == 1, otherwise, team j is stronger than team i.
Team a will be the champion of the tournament if there is no team b that is stronger than team a.
Return the team that will be the champion of the tournament.
 
Example 1:

Input: grid = [[0,1],[0,0]]
Output: 0
Explanation: There are two teams in this tournament.
grid[0][1] == 1 means that team 0 is stronger than team 1. So team 0 will be the champion.

Example 2:

Input: grid = [[0,0,1],[1,0,1],[0,0,0]]
Output: 1
Explanation: There are three teams in this tournament.
grid[1][0] == 1 means that team 1 is stronger than team 0.
grid[1][2] == 1 means that team 1 is stronger than team 2.
So team 1 will be the champion.

 
Constraints:

n == grid.length
n == grid[i].length
2 <= n <= 100
grid[i][j] is either 0 or 1.
For all i grid[i][i] is 0.
For all i, j that i != j, grid[i][j] != grid[j][i].
The input is generated such that if team a is stronger than team b and team b is stronger than team c, then team a is stronger than team c.
```

### Starter Code

```python
class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
```

## Generation

### System Prompt

```text
You are an expert Python programmer. You will be given a question (problem specification) and will generate a correct Python program that matches the specification and passes all tests.
```

### User Prompt

```text
### Question:
There are n teams numbered from 0 to n - 1 in a tournament.
Given a 0-indexed 2D boolean matrix grid of size n * n. For all i, j that 0 <= i, j <= n - 1 and i != j team i is stronger than team j if grid[i][j] == 1, otherwise, team j is stronger than team i.
Team a will be the champion of the tournament if there is no team b that is stronger than team a.
Return the team that will be the champion of the tournament.
 
Example 1:

Input: grid = [[0,1],[0,0]]
Output: 0
Explanation: There are two teams in this tournament.
grid[0][1] == 1 means that team 0 is stronger than team 1. So team 0 will be the champion.

Example 2:

Input: grid = [[0,0,1],[1,0,1],[0,0,0]]
Output: 1
Explanation: There are three teams in this tournament.
grid[1][0] == 1 means that team 1 is stronger than team 0.
grid[1][2] == 1 means that team 1 is stronger than team 2.
So team 1 will be the champion.

 
Constraints:

n == grid.length
n == grid[i].length
2 <= n <= 100
grid[i][j] is either 0 or 1.
For all i grid[i][i] is 0.
For all i, j that i != j, grid[i][j] != grid[j][i].
The input is generated such that if team a is stronger than team b and team b is stronger than team c, then team a is stronger than team c.

### Format: You will use the following starter code to write the solution to the problem and enclose your code within delimiters.
```python
class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        
```

### Answer: (use the provided format with backticks)
```

### Outputs

<details>
<summary>Generation 1</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0

        # Find a potential champion candidate
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If i is stronger than current champion, i becomes new candidate
            if grid[i][champion] == 1:
                champion = i

        # Verify candidate: it must be stronger than everyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[champion][j] != 1:
                return -1  # should not happen with valid inputs

        return champion
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Generation 2</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        # Candidate elimination: if i is weaker than j, i cannot be champion.
        cand = 0
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[cand][i] == 1:   # cand beats i => keep cand
                continue
            cand = i                # cand loses to i => i becomes new candidate

        # Verify candidate is stronger than everyone else.
        for j in range(n):
            if j == cand:
                continue
            if grid[cand][j] != 1:  # cand must beat j
                return -1  # should not happen per problem guarantees
        return cand
```
```

</details>

<summary>Generation 3</summary>

```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        for i in range(n):
            # team i is champion if no other team is stronger than it
            # i.e., for every j != i, grid[j][i] must be 0
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:
                    break
            else:
                return i
        return -1  # should not happen due to problem guarantees
```
```

```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0
        
        # Eliminate teams that cannot be champion
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If current candidate is beaten by i, then candidate can't be champion
            if grid[i][candidate] == 1:
                candidate = i
        
        # Verify candidate beats every other team
        for j in range(n):
            if j == candidate:
                continue
            if grid[candidate][j] == 0:  # j beats candidate
                return -1
        return candidate
```
```

```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        for i in range(n):
            champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:  # someone stronger than i
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return i
        return -1
```

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        for i in range(n):
            # team i is champion if for every other j, grid[i][j] == 1
            # (meaning i is stronger than j)
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[i][j] == 0:
                    break
            else:
                return i
        return -1  # should never happen given problem constraints

from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)

        for a in range(n):
            champion = True
            for b in range(n):
                if a == b:
                    continue
                # if b is stronger than a, then a can't be champion
                # b is stronger than a iff grid[b][a] == 1
                if grid[b][a] == 1:
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return a

        return -1  # should never happen given the problem constraints
```
```

<summary>Generation 9</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0

        # Eliminate all teams that cannot be the champion.
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If current champion is stronger than i (grid[champion][i] == 1),
            # keep champion; otherwise i becomes the only possible champion.
            if grid[champion][i] == 0:
                champion = i

        # Verify champion: it must be stronger than every other team.
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[champion][j] == 0:
                return -1  # not expected by problem constraints
        return champion
```
```

```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0

        # Eliminate teams that cannot be champions.
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[candidate][i] == 1:
                # candidate is stronger than i -> i can't beat candidate
                continue
            else:
                # i is stronger than candidate -> candidate can't be champion
                candidate = i

        # Verify candidate is not weaker than any other team.
        for j in range(n):
            if j != candidate and grid[j][candidate] == 1:
                return -1  # someone stronger than candidate exists

        return candidate
```
```

</details>

## Memory

- Skipped: `true`
- Reason: `insufficient_tiers`

### Grouped Solutions

#### Tier: `full`

<details>
<summary>full attempt 1</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0

        # Find a potential champion candidate
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If i is stronger than current champion, i becomes new candidate
            if grid[i][champion] == 1:
                champion = i

        # Verify candidate: it must be stronger than everyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[champion][j] != 1:
                return -1  # should not happen with valid inputs

        return champion
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 2</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        # Candidate elimination: if i is weaker than j, i cannot be champion.
        cand = 0
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[cand][i] == 1:   # cand beats i => keep cand
                continue
            cand = i                # cand loses to i => i becomes new candidate

        # Verify candidate is stronger than everyone else.
        for j in range(n):
            if j == cand:
                continue
            if grid[cand][j] != 1:  # cand must beat j
                return -1  # should not happen per problem guarantees
        return cand
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 3</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        for i in range(n):
            # team i is champion if no other team is stronger than it
            # i.e., for every j != i, grid[j][i] must be 0
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:
                    break
            else:
                return i
        return -1  # should not happen due to problem guarantees
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 4</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0
        
        # Eliminate teams that cannot be champion
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If current candidate is beaten by i, then candidate can't be champion
            if grid[i][candidate] == 1:
                candidate = i
        
        # Verify candidate beats every other team
        for j in range(n):
            if j == candidate:
                continue
            if grid[candidate][j] == 0:  # j beats candidate
                return -1
        return candidate
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 5</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        for i in range(n):
            champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:  # someone stronger than i
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return i
        return -1
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 6</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        for i in range(n):
            # team i is champion if for every other j, grid[i][j] == 1
            # (meaning i is stronger than j)
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[i][j] == 0:
                    break
            else:
                return i
        return -1  # should never happen given problem constraints
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 7</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        
        for a in range(n):
            champion = True
            for b in range(n):
                if a != b and grid[b][a] == 1:  # someone stronger than a exists
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return a
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 8</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)

        for a in range(n):
            champion = True
            for b in range(n):
                if a == b:
                    continue
                # if b is stronger than a, then a can't be champion
                # b is stronger than a iff grid[b][a] == 1
                if grid[b][a] == 1:
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return a

        return -1  # should never happen given the problem constraints
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 9</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0

        # Eliminate all teams that cannot be the champion.
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If current champion is stronger than i (grid[champion][i] == 1),
            # keep champion; otherwise i becomes the only possible champion.
            if grid[champion][i] == 0:
                champion = i

        # Verify champion: it must be stronger than every other team.
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[champion][j] == 0:
                return -1  # not expected by problem constraints
        return champion
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>full attempt 10</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0

        # Eliminate teams that cannot be champions.
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[candidate][i] == 1:
                # candidate is stronger than i -> i can't beat candidate
                continue
            else:
                # i is stronger than candidate -> candidate can't be champion
                candidate = i

        # Verify candidate is not weaker than any other team.
        for j in range(n):
            if j != candidate and grid[j][candidate] == 1:
                return -1  # someone stronger than candidate exists

        return candidate
```
```

### Baseline

### System Prompt

```text
You are an expert Python programmer. You will be given a question (problem specification) and will generate a correct Python program that matches the specification and passes all tests.
```

### User Prompt

```text
### Question:
There are n teams numbered from 0 to n - 1 in a tournament.
Given a 0-indexed 2D boolean matrix grid of size n * n. For all i, j that 0 <= i, j <= n - 1 and i != j team i is stronger than team j if grid[i][j] == 1, otherwise, team j is stronger than team i.
Team a will be the champion of the tournament if there is no team b that is stronger than team a.
Return the team that will be the champion of the tournament.
 
Example 1:

Input: grid = [[0,1],[0,0]]
Output: 0
Explanation: There are two teams in this tournament.
grid[0][1] == 1 means that team 0 is stronger than team 1. So team 0 will be the champion.

Example 2:

Input: grid = [[0,0,1],[1,0,1],[0,0,0]]
Output: 1
Explanation: There are three teams in this tournament.
grid[1][0] == 1 means that team 1 is stronger than team 0.
grid[1][2] == 1 means that team 1 is stronger than team 2.
So team 1 will be the champion.

 
Constraints:

n == grid.length
n == grid[i].length
2 <= n <= 100
grid[i][j] is either 0 or 1.
For all i grid[i][i] is 0.
For all i, j that i != j, grid[i][j] != grid[j][i].
The input is generated such that if team a is stronger than team b and team b is stronger than team c, then team a is stronger than team c.

### Format: You will use the following starter code to write the solution to the problem and enclose your code within delimiters.
```python
class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        
```

### Answer: (use the provided format with backticks)
```

#### Outputs

<details>
<summary>Baseline generation 1</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0
        # Elimination tournament: if i loses to current candidate, discard candidate.
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[champion][i] == 0:  # i is stronger than champion
                champion = i

        # Verify champion beats everyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[champion][j] == 0:
                return -1  # In valid inputs, a champion should always exist.

        return champion
```
```

<details>
<summary>Baseline generation 2</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        # In a total order (tournament + transitive), the champion is the one
        # such that no other team is stronger than it.
        for i in range(n):
            champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:  # someone j is stronger than i
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return i
        return -1  # Should never happen given constraints
```
```

from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0

        # Pick a possible champion by elimination
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If candidate is weaker than i, i becomes the new candidate
            if grid[candidate][i] == 0:
                candidate = i

        # Verify candidate is not weaker than anyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != candidate and grid[candidate][j] == 0:
                return -1  # Shouldn't happen due to problem guarantee

        return candidate

from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        
        # Team i is champion iff for every other team j, grid[j][i] == 1 (j stronger than i is impossible)
        for i in range(n):
            is_champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:
                    is_champion = False
                    break
            if is_champion:
                return i
        
        # Problem guarantees a champion exists
        return -1
```

<summary>Baseline generation 5</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0
        
        # Find a possible champion by elimination.
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If current candidate loses to i, i becomes the new candidate.
            if grid[candidate][i] == 0:  # grid[i][candidate] must be 1 due to consistency
                candidate = i
        
        # Verify candidate beats everyone else.
        for j in range(n):
            if j == candidate:
                continue
            if grid[candidate][j] == 0:  # candidate does not beat j
                return -1  # per problem constraints, this shouldn't happen
        
        return candidate
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Baseline generation 6</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidates = set(range(n))
        
        for i in range(n):
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[i][j] == 1:  # i is stronger than j
                    if j in candidates:
                        candidates.remove(j)
        
        # Exactly one team remains as champion; return it
        return next(iter(candidates))
```
```

</details>

```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0

        # Eliminate non-champions via pairwise comparison
        for i in range(1, n):
            # if current i is stronger than champion, replace
            if grid[i][champion] == 1:
                champion = i

        # Verify champion beats everyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[j][champion] == 1:
                return -1  # should not happen with given guarantees

        return champion
```

from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0

        # Find a possible champion by pairwise elimination:
        # If candidate is weaker than i, then candidate cannot be champion.
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[candidate][i] == 0:  # grid[candidate][i] == 0 => i is stronger
                candidate = i

        # Verify candidate: it must beat everyone else.
        for j in range(n):
            if j != candidate and grid[candidate][j] == 0:
                return -1  # should not happen given problem guarantees

        return candidate
```

<summary>Baseline generation 9</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        # A champion is a team with no incoming "stronger than" edges.
        # grid[i][j] == 1 means i is stronger than j, so champion a must have
        # grid[b][a] == 0 for all b != a.
        for a in range(n):
            is_champion = True
            for b in range(n):
                if b != a and grid[b][a] == 1:
                    is_champion = False
                    break
            if is_champion:
                return a
        return -1  # Should never happen under valid tournament constraints.
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Baseline generation 10</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)

        # A team i is the champion iff for every other team j, grid[j][i] == 1.
        for i in range(n):
            champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i == j:
                    continue
                if grid[j][i] != 1:  # some team j is not weaker than i
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return i

        # Problem guarantees there is always exactly one champion in such inputs.
        return -1
```
```

### Augmented

<details>
<summary>Augmented generation 1</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0
        # Elimination tournament: if i loses to current candidate, discard candidate.
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[champion][i] == 0:  # i is stronger than champion
                champion = i

        # Verify champion beats everyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[champion][j] == 0:
                return -1  # In valid inputs, a champion should always exist.

        return champion
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Augmented generation 2</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        # In a total order (tournament + transitive), the champion is the one
        # such that no other team is stronger than it.
        for i in range(n):
            champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:  # someone j is stronger than i
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return i
        return -1  # Should never happen given constraints
```
```

</details>

<summary>Augmented generation 3</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0

        # Pick a possible champion by elimination
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If candidate is weaker than i, i becomes the new candidate
            if grid[candidate][i] == 0:
                candidate = i

        # Verify candidate is not weaker than anyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != candidate and grid[candidate][j] == 0:
                return -1  # Shouldn't happen due to problem guarantee

        return candidate
```
```

</details>

<summary>Augmented generation 4</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        
        # Team i is champion iff for every other team j, grid[j][i] == 1 (j stronger than i is impossible)
        for i in range(n):
            is_champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[j][i] == 1:
                    is_champion = False
                    break
            if is_champion:
                return i
        
        # Problem guarantees a champion exists
        return -1
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Augmented generation 5</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0
        
        # Find a possible champion by elimination.
        for i in range(1, n):
            # If current candidate loses to i, i becomes the new candidate.
            if grid[candidate][i] == 0:  # grid[i][candidate] must be 1 due to consistency
                candidate = i
        
        # Verify candidate beats everyone else.
        for j in range(n):
            if j == candidate:
                continue
            if grid[candidate][j] == 0:  # candidate does not beat j
                return -1  # per problem constraints, this shouldn't happen
        
        return candidate
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Augmented generation 6</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidates = set(range(n))
        
        for i in range(n):
            for j in range(n):
                if i != j and grid[i][j] == 1:  # i is stronger than j
                    if j in candidates:
                        candidates.remove(j)
        
        # Exactly one team remains as champion; return it
        return next(iter(candidates))
```
```

</details>

<summary>Augmented generation 7</summary>

```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        champion = 0

        # Eliminate non-champions via pairwise comparison
        for i in range(1, n):
            # if current i is stronger than champion, replace
            if grid[i][champion] == 1:
                champion = i

        # Verify champion beats everyone else
        for j in range(n):
            if j != champion and grid[j][champion] == 1:
                return -1  # should not happen with given guarantees

        return champion
```
```

<summary>Augmented generation 8</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        candidate = 0

        # Find a possible champion by pairwise elimination:
        # If candidate is weaker than i, then candidate cannot be champion.
        for i in range(1, n):
            if grid[candidate][i] == 0:  # grid[candidate][i] == 0 => i is stronger
                candidate = i

        # Verify candidate: it must beat everyone else.
        for j in range(n):
            if j != candidate and grid[candidate][j] == 0:
                return -1  # should not happen given problem guarantees

        return candidate
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Augmented generation 9</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)
        # A champion is a team with no incoming "stronger than" edges.
        # grid[i][j] == 1 means i is stronger than j, so champion a must have
        # grid[b][a] == 0 for all b != a.
        for a in range(n):
            is_champion = True
            for b in range(n):
                if b != a and grid[b][a] == 1:
                    is_champion = False
                    break
            if is_champion:
                return a
        return -1  # Should never happen under valid tournament constraints.
```
```

</details>

<details>
<summary>Augmented generation 10</summary>

```text
```python
from typing import List

class Solution:
    def findChampion(self, grid: List[List[int]]) -> int:
        n = len(grid)

        # A team i is the champion iff for every other team j, grid[j][i] == 1.
        for i in range(n):
            champion = True
            for j in range(n):
                if i == j:
                    continue
                if grid[j][i] != 1:  # some team j is not weaker than i
                    champion = False
                    break
            if champion:
                return i

        # Problem guarantees there is always exactly one champion in such inputs.
        return -1
```
```
